        "import pandas as pd\n",
        "from openpyxl import Workbook\n",
        "from openpyxl.utils.dataframe import dataframe_to_rows\n",
        "\n",
        "wb = Workbook()\n",
        "ws = wb.active\n",
        "ws.title = \"Sheet1\"\n",
        "\n",
        "# Split data into chunks of 10 rows\n",
        "chunks = [df[i:i + 10] for i in range(0, df.shape[0], 10)]\n",
        "\n",
        "# Print the data before writing to Excel\n",
        "print(\"Data in DataFrame:\")\n",
        "print(df) # This will print the entire DataFrame to the console\n",
        "\n",
        "# Write data to sheets\n",
        "for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks):\n",
        "    if i > 0:  # Create new sheets for subsequent chunks\n",
        "        ws = wb.create_sheet(f\"Sheet{i+1}\")\n",
        "    # Only include header in first sheet\n",
        "    for r in dataframe_to_rows(chunk, index=False, header=True if i == 0 else False):\n",
        "        ws.append(r)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Save the workbook\n",
        "wb.save(\"output.xlsx\")"

        "for script in soup([\"script\", \"style\"]): # remove all javascript and stylesheet code\n",
        "  script.extract()\n",
        "# get text\n",
        "text = soup.get_text()\n",
        "# break into lines and remove leading and trail\n",
        "\n",
        "lines = (line.strip() for line in text.splitlines())\n",
        "# break multi-headlines into a line each\n",
        "chunks = (phrase.strip() for line in lines for phrase in line.split(\" \"))\n",
        "# drop blank lines\n",
        "texts = '\\n'.join(chunk for chunk in chunks if chunk)\n",
        "print(texts)"

      "source": [
        "import requests\n",
        "from bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n",
        "import os\n",
        "from google.colab import drive\n",
        "# 挂载 Google Drive（可选，如果需要保存到云端硬盘）\n",
        "drive.mount('/content/drive')\n",
        "# 定义并创建保存图片的目录\n",
        "save_dir = '/content/drive/MyDrive/ Notebooks/download/'\n",
        "if not os.path.exists(save_dir):\n",
        "  os.makedirs(save_dir)\n",
        "web = requests.get('https://www.ptt.cc/bbs/Beauty/M.1710593264.A.578.html',\n",
        "cookies={'over18':'1'})\n",
        "soup = BeautifulSoup(web.text, \"html.parser\")\n",
        "imgs = soup.find_all('img')\n",
        "name = 0 # 设定图片编号\n",
        "for i in imgs:\n",
        "  print(i['src'])\n",
        "  jpg = requests.get(i['src']) # 使用 requests 获取图片内容\n",
        "  with open(f'{save_dir}test_{name}.jpg', 'wb') as f:\n",
        "    f.write(jpg.content) # 写入图片内容\n",
        "  name += 1 # 编号增加 1"
      ],

            "              <div class=\"etw-bgbox_inner\" style=\"line-height: 160%;\">\n",
            "                <h3 class=\"etw-boxtitle etw-color-browndark mb-3\">領獎注意事項</h3>\n",
            "                \n",
            "                  <div>\n",
            "<p>1.領獎期間自113年10月6日起至114年1月6日止，中獎人請於領獎期間攜帶國民身分證(非本國國籍人士得以護照、居留證或內政部移民署核發入出境許可證等替代)及中獎統一發票，依代發獎金單位公告之兌獎營業時間臨櫃兌領，逾期不得領獎。<br />2.統一發票未依規定載明金額者，不得領獎。<br />3.統一發票買受人為政府機關、公營事業、公立學校、部隊及營業人者，不得領獎。<br />4.中三獎(含)以上者，依規定應由發獎單位扣繳20﹪所得稅款。<br />5.中五獎 及雲端發票專屬獎500元（含）以上者，依規定應繳納0.4%印花稅款，但已於財政部電子發票整合服務平台或統一發票兌獎APP設定領獎帳戶兌領獎金者，免繳納印花稅。<br />6.中獎之統一發票如同時對中多數獎項，以兌領一個獎項為限。<br />7.詳細領獎規定，請查閱「統一發票給獎辦法」。若有疑義，請洽財金公司客服專線：4128282(手機請撥：02-4128282)，或至財金公司網站查詢。&nbsp; &nbsp;</p>\n",
            "</div>\n",

        "import requests\n",
        "url = 'https://invoice.etax.nat.gov.tw/index.html'\n",
        "web = requests.get(url) # 取得網頁內容\n",
        "web.encoding='utf-8' # 因為該網頁編碼為 utf-8，加上 .encoding 避免亂碼\n",
        "from bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n",
        "soup = BeautifulSoup(web.text, \"html.parser\") # 轉換成標籤樹\n",
        "td = soup.select('.container-fluid')[0].select('.etw-tbiggest') #取出中獎號碼的位置\n",
        "ns = td[0].getText() # 特別獎\n",
